## [人工饲养双胞胎狮宝宝满月](https://m.weibo.cn/search?containerid=100103type%3D1%26t%3D10%26q%3D%23%E4%BA%BA%E5%B7%A5%E9%A5%B2%E5%85%BB%E5%8F%8C%E8%83%9E%E8%83%8E%E7%8B%AE%E5%AE%9D%E5%AE%9D%E6%BB%A1%E6%9C%88%23&isnewpage=1&extparam=seat%3D1%26filter_type%3Drealtimehot%26dgr%3D0%26cate%3D0%26pos%3D47%26realpos%3D47%26flag%3D0%26c_type%3D31%26display_time%3D1625418341%26pre_seqid%3D1625418341448017712148&luicode=10000011&lfid=106003type%3D25%26t%3D3%26disable_hot%3D1%26filter_type%3Drealtimehot) `社会` 
 日前，重庆乐和乐都野生动物世界一只非洲狮产下双胞胎幼崽。由于狮妈妈年龄偏大，加之习性暴躁，在产下两只狮宝宝后，不久便不再哺乳幼崽。饲养员只能采取人工喂养方式养育两个小家伙。
